		icon = GFX_decision_eng_trade_unions_support

				AND = {
					has_war_with = FRA

						is_in_faction = yes
						is_subject = no
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = great_war_loser
						}
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_war_with = ENG

						is_in_faction = yes

							has_country_flag = great_war_loser
						}
					}
				}
			}
			has_global_flag = great_war
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = great_war_loser
				has_global_flag = great_war_ends
				has_global_flag = GER_capitulation
				has_global_flag = FRA_capitulation
				has_global_flag = mudros_armistice
			}
			surrender_progress > 0.19
			OR = {
				# Constantinople lost
				AND = {
					owns_state = 347
					NOT = { controls_state = 347 }
				}	
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						has_war_with = RUS
					}	
					OR = {						
						surrender_progress > 0.39
						# Constantinople threatened

							OR = {
								controls_state = 341
								controls_state = 825

						}			
					}

			controls_state = 347
			surrender_progress < 0.20

					NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				}
			}

	TUR_invoke_senussiya_alliance = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_nationalism
		allowed = {
			original_tag = TUR
		}
		fire_only_once = yes
		visible = {
			has_global_flag = great_war
			is_subject = no
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = great_war_ends
			}
			FROM = {
				is_subject = no
				is_in_faction = no
				OR = {
					has_government = neutrality
					has_government = fascism
				}	
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = TUR
					has_war_together_with = TUR
					has_country_flag = LBA_modus_vivendi_of_acroma
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					LBA = {
						is_ai = no
					}
				}
				is_in_faction = yes
			}	
		}
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				tag = LBA
			}
		}
		available = {
			has_war = yes
			any_country = {
				has_war_with = TUR
				any_owned_state = {
					is_core_of = LBA
				}
			}
		}
		days_remove = 14
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					LBA = {
						is_ai = yes				
					}
				}				
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						has_war_with = TUR
						any_owned_state = {
							is_core_of = LBA
						}
					}
					LBA = {
						add_to_war = {
							targeted_alliance = TUR
							enemy = PREV
						}	
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_in_faction = yes	
					}
					add_to_faction = LBA
				}
				else = {
					LBA = {
						country_event = generic.5
					}
				}
			}	
			LBA = {
				set_country_flag = TUR_invoke_senussiya_alliance
			}	
		}
		cost = 15
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 15
			modifier = {
				has_war_with = ITA
				factor = 1000
			}
			modifier = {
				date < 1915.11.1
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}
}

			has_country_flag = TUR_can_send_armenians_to_the_east
			controls_state = FROM
			FROM = {
				has_state_flag = TUR_assyrian_state
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_assyrian_minority }
			}
		}
		available = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					country_exists = ARM
					ARM = {
						any_owned_state = {
							is_core_of = ARM
						}
					}
				}
				any_state = {
					NOT = {
						is_owned_by = TUR
						is_controlled_by = TUR
					}
					is_core_of = ARM
				}
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			FROM = {
				set_temp_variable = {
					TUR.TUR_target_state_manpower = state_population
				}
				divide_temp_variable = {
					TUR.TUR_target_state_manpower = -5
				}
				add_manpower = var:TUR.TUR_target_state_manpower
				if = {
					limit = {
						country_exists = ARM
					}
					random_state = {
						limit = {
							is_owned_and_controlled_by = ARM
							is_core_of = ARM
							has_state_flag = TUR_armenian_state_legacy
						}
						divide_temp_variable = {
							TUR.TUR_target_state_manpower = -1
						}
						add_manpower = var:TUR.TUR_target_state_manpower
					}
				}
				else = {
					random_state = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { is_owned_by = TUR }
							NOT = { is_controlled_by = TUR }
							is_core_of = ARM
						}
						divide_temp_variable = {
							TUR.TUR_target_state_manpower = -1
						}
						add_manpower = var:TUR.TUR_target_state_manpower
					}
				}
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			FROM = {
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_assyrian_minority }
				clr_state_flag = TUR_assyrian_state
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							is_core_of = TUR
						}
					}
					add_core_of = TUR
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = ASY
						state = 828
					}
					remove_core_of = ASY
					set_state_flag = TUR_no_longer_assyria_core_tt
				}
				set_state_flag = TUR_unintended_consequence_relocate_armenians_to_east
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = TUR_relocate_armenians_to_the_east_flag
					}
					add_dynamic_modifier = {
						modifier = TUR_breakdown_of_economic_infrastructure
						days = 180
					}
				}
				ottoman_minority_variable_check = yes
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				FROM = {
					any_neighbor_state = {
						has_state_flag = TUR_ottoman_minority_state
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				FROM = {
					any_neighbor_state = {
						any_country = {
							has_war_with = TUR
							controls_state = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

TUR_army_modernization = {
	TUR_army_modernization_decision = {
		allowed = {
			tag = TUR
		}
		icon = generic_army_support
		custom_cost_text = TUR_decision_cost_armyxp
		custom_cost_trigger = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = TUR_import_foreign_advisors
				}
				has_army_experience > 9.99
			}
			else = {
				has_army_experience > 29.99
			}
		}
		fire_only_once = no
		days_remove = 15
		days_re_enable = 70
		visible = {
			OR = {
				has_completed_focus = TUR_import_foreign_advisors
				has_completed_focus = TUR_damascus_maneuvers
			}
			TUR_has_army_of_a_bygone_era = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			experience_gain_army_factor = -0.15
		}
		complete_effect = {
			TUR_modernize_army_effect = yes
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_completed_focus = TUR_import_foreign_advisors
					}
					army_experience = -10
				}
				else = {
					army_experience = -30
				}
			}
		}
		cancel_if_not_visible = no
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				date > 1912.1.1
			}
		}
	}
	TUR_navy_modernization_decision = {
		allowed = {
			tag = TUR
		}

		}

TUR_reclaiming_ahd_i_milli = {
	TUR_border_skirmishes = {
		icon = border_war

		target_array = neighbors

		available = {
			FROM = {
				any_owned_state = {
					is_controlled_by = FROM
					any_neighbor_state = {
						is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
						set_temp_variable = { var:attacker_state_temp = id }
						has_ROOT_at_least_1_div_in_current_state_scope = yes
						hidden_trigger = { NOT = { has_state_flag = border_incident_active } }
					}
					NOT = { has_state_flag = border_incident_active }
					set_temp_variable = { var:defender_state_temp = id }
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_non_aggression_pact_with = FROM }
		}

		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = TUR_disobey_the_treaties
			FROM = { exists = yes }
			NOT = { has_war_with = FROM }
			FROM = { has_not_initiated_border_incident_with_ROOT = yes }
			FROM = {
				NOT = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				is_subject_of = FROM
			}

			NOT = { has_border_war_with = FROM }
			FROM = {
				any_owned_state = {
					OR = {
						is_claimed_by = ROOT
						is_core_of = ROOT
					}
					hidden_trigger = { NOT = { has_state_flag = border_incident_active } }
					any_neighbor_state = {
						hidden_trigger = { NOT = { has_state_flag = border_incident_active } }
						is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 0
		}

		cost = 50

		fire_only_once = no

		days_remove = 7
		days_re_enable = 15

		complete_effect = {
			hidden_effect = {
				FROM = {
					random_owned_controlled_state = {
						limit = {
							is_claimed_by = ROOT
							hidden_trigger = { NOT = { has_state_flag = border_incident_active } }
							any_neighbor_state = {
								hidden_trigger = { NOT = { has_state_flag = border_incident_active } }
								has_ROOT_at_least_1_div_in_current_state_scope = yes
								is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
							}
						}
						save_event_target_as = defender_state
						set_variable = { FROM.defender_state_vs_@ROOT = id }
						set_temp_variable = { defender_state_temp = id }
						set_state_flag = border_incident_active
					}
				}
				random_state = {
					limit = {
						is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
						hidden_trigger = { NOT = { has_state_flag = border_incident_active } }
						has_ROOT_at_least_1_div_in_current_state_scope = yes
						any_neighbor_state = {
							state = var:FROM.defender_state_vs_@ROOT
						}
					}
					save_event_target_as = attacker_state
					set_variable = { FROM.attacker_state_vs_@ROOT = id }
					set_temp_variable = { attacker_state_temp = id }
					set_state_flag = border_incident_active
				}
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			start_border_war = {
				change_state_after_war = yes
				attacker = {
					state = var:FROM.attacker_state_vs_@ROOT
					num_provinces = 4
					on_win = wtt_border_conflict_won_attacker.1
					on_lose = wtt_border_conflict_lost_attacker.1
					on_cancel = wtt_border_conflict_canceled_attacker.1
				}
				
				defender = {
					state = var:FROM.defender_state_vs_@ROOT
					num_provinces = 4
					on_win = wtt_border_conflict_won_defender.1
					on_lose = wtt_border_conflict_lost_defender.1
					on_cancel = wtt_border_conflict_canceled_defender.1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_border_conflict_defender_vs_FROM = yes }
				var:attacker_state_vs_@FROM = {
					clr_state_flag = border_incident_active
				}
				var:defender_state_vs_@FROM = {
					clr_state_flag = border_incident_active
				}
				clear_variable = attacker_state_vs_@FROM
				clear_variable = defender_state_vs_@FROM
			}
			else = {
				FROM = {
					var:attacker_state_vs_@ROOT = {
						clr_state_flag = border_incident_active
					}
					var:defender_state_vs_@ROOT = {
						clr_state_flag = border_incident_active
					}
					clear_variable = attacker_state_vs_@ROOT
					clear_variable = defender_state_vs_@ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		icon = GFX_decision_generic_nationalism
		allowed = { 
			original_tag = TUR
		}
		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = TUR_call_to_the_world

				}
			}
			any_state = {
				is_controlled_by = FROM
				is_core_of = FROM
				is_in_home_area = yes
			}
		}
		cost = 50
		available = {
			has_equipment = {
				infantry_equipment > 1499
			}

				is_owned_by = FROM
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}

					}
				}

			}
		}
		fire_only_once = no

			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						check_variable = { num_of_controlled_states = 1 }
					}
				}
				FROM = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = communism

					}

						country_event = ottoman.197
					}
				}
			}

				FROM = {
					add_to_temp_variable = {
						var = civil_war_size_var
						value = party_popularity@communism
					}
					start_civil_war = {
						ideology = communism
						size = civil_war_size_var
						keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
							OR = {
								has_trait = trait_royal
								has_trait = trait_royalist
								has_trait = old_guard
								has_trait = old_guard_navy
								has_trait = politically_connected
							}
						}
					}
					hidden_effect = {
						country_event = ottoman.197
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
